Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: ............19 ( (various owners) ) THISfirstentryinSignificantShipsfromoneofKorea'smallershipyards, basedinthesouth-coastportofTongyoung, isoneofthreesistershipsorderedbyQatarShippingfromastandard37,00dwtchemical/productankerdesigndevelopedinShina’sowntechnicaldepartments, andwhichasalreadyattractedasubstantialnumberofordersfromvariousowners. Alnomanisasingle-deckedvesselwithaforecastlewhichislinkedtothedeckhouseaftbymeansofaforeandaftgangwaybuiltabovethedeck.
TosuitlengthrestrictionsinforceinmanyEuropeanandAmericanterminalports, Shinahasoptedtobaseitsdesignona175.90moverallength, whilst, athesametimensuringPanamaCanalnavigationwithabeamof31.00m.
Alnomanhasbeenconstructedwithlessthan30% high-tensilesteelandcomplieswiththelatestinternationalrulesandregulations, includingExxonrequirements. Amongstechnicalequipmentonboardisavoyagedatarecorder. CargoesclassifiedasIMOTypeII canbecarriedinacargospacecontainedwithinadouble-skinhull, dividedbyacentreline, andsixtransversebulkheads, into12cargotanks, twosloptanksandoneresidualstank. Allarefinishedwithaphenol-epoxycoatingappliedtoaplainsurface, sinceallsteelworkstiffening, includingdeckbeams, isfittedoutsidethetanks.
TheTypeII rangeofcargoesincludescausticsodandmolasses, andtheFrankMohn, hydraulicallyoperated, submergedpumpsfittedintoeachtank, togetherwithpipeworkandfittings, areofstainlessteelconstructiontosuitheseproducts. Cargoishandledthroughmidshipmanifoldsportandstarboard, servedbya10tonneswl, electro-hydraulichose- handlingcrane, withdischargealsopossibleoverthesternbymeansofa300mmline.
ThemainengineisanMANB&W6S50MCunitbuiltbyHSD, havinganMCRoutputof8580kWat127rev/minandrivingafour-bladedpropellerof5750mmdiameter. Despitehavingablockcoefficientofaround0.80, thisclassoftankerisdesignedforaservicespeedof15knotsat90% MCRandwitha15% seamargin. Electricalsupplycomesfromthree740kWTaiyoalternatorsfittedwithSTX (Ssangyong) dieselprimemovers, andsteamrequirementsareservedbyanAalborgoil-firedboiler. Unusuallyforthistypeofvessel, a 'flap-type' rudderisfitted, withmanoeuvringfurtherenhancedbyaKawasaki950kWbowthruster.

Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder:................4 ( (plus 4 options) ) Illustrationshows8234-classprototypeNorasiaValparaisoDESPITEtheconomicdifficultiesofthepastyear, theGdyniaShipyardmanagedtokeepitsbuildingprogrammemovingtosomedegree, withtheresulthatafterseveralmonthsdelay, itwasfinallypossibletoresumeconstructionofwhatareunderstoodtobethelargestandfastestcontainershipsyetbuiltinPoland, withacapacityof444TEU. Basedonanearlierdesignfora400TEUvessel, this8234serieshasbeenupgradedtosuitheowner'srequirementsforstabilityintakeandsustainedspeed, byincreasingshiplengthandfittingamorepowerfulengine. AnewhullformwastestedatheGdanskModelBasin, withparticularattentiongiventopropellerdesign, shapeofrudder (whichincludesthefittingofabulb), andarrangementandsizeofbilgekeels. Thisalsopresentsanalmostcompletelyrectangularupperdeck - narrowedonlyathebow. Thedouble-skinhullenclosesevencargoholdsforwardofthemachineryroom, withonesmallholdunderthedeckaft, uponwhichthreeFEUstackscanbestowed.
Thehatchesareclosedbyweathertightpontooncoversofopenconstruction, andtheirlongitudinaldispositionallowswiderspacingbetweencontainerbaysthaninother, competitivedesigns, facilitatinglashingaccessandprovidingspaceforlashingbridges.
Electricalconnectionsareprovidedondeckfor450refrigeratedFEUtobecarried, witharrangementsmadeforthefutureinstallationofadditionalventilationintheholdsifoptionalreeferpositionsareutilised.
Thestabilitycharacteristicsofthedesignhavebeenenhancedbyoptimisedtanksubdivision, withthedoublebottomarrangementlaidoutwithoutacentralduct-keel. Theforeandaftaccesspassages, normallyfoundinthe 'tweendeck' abovethesidetanksinthistypeofvessel, havebeeneliminated, andthetanksextendedtoupperdeckleveltoimprovedamagestability. Aneight-tierdeckhouseispositionedabovetheupperdeck, providingaline-of-sightoverthemaximumseventiersofcontainerswhichcanbeloaded. Itsheightalsoensuresthatanowner'srequirementfora51.80mairdraughtabovekeelcanbemaintained. Forthisreasonalso, thesignalmastabovethebridgeisarrangedtofold.
KoreanbuilderHyundaiHeavyIndustriesuppliedtheSulzer8RTA96Cmainengine, whichdevelops43,920kWat100rev/min, tobtainaservicespeedof24.90knotsat90% fullpowerandallowing15% seamargin, fromtheFPpropeller, designedandmanufacturedbyStoneManganeseMarine. Thefouralternatorsets, twoeachof2250kVAand200kVArating, havebeensuppliedbyAvanKaick, andarefittedwithMANB&Wprimemovers, withcontrolbyapowermanagementsystem, whichformspartofanautomationandcontrolpackagedesignedbySTNAtlasMarine (SAM) Electronics. Controlofengineroomequipmentiscarriedoutfromashipoperatingcentreinthedeckhouse, usinganintegratedautomationsystem (IAS) performingallalarm, controlandmonitoringfunctions.

Shipbuilder: : . .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .Barkmeijer Stroobos BV, , The Netherlands
Vessel'sname: :. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .Arklow River
Hullnumber: : . .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .300
Owner/operator: :. .. .. .. .. .Arklow Shipping Ltd, , Ireland
Designer: :. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .Barkmeijer Stroobos/ / Conoship International, , The Netherlands
Flag: : . .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .Ireland Totalnumberofsistershipsalreadycompleted: :. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .1 Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: : . .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .. .5 ARKLOWRiverformspartofanewclassofcirca- 4500dwtvesselscurrentlybeingdeliveredfromtheBarkmeijeryard, andbuiltoadesignwhichsharesmanyfeatureswithtwosistershipscompletedin2002byfellowConoshipmember, ShipyardBijlsma (Arklow
Rally: SignificantShipsof2002). Althoughofsimilardimensionstothosevessels, ArklowRiverdoesdifferbyhavingspecificarrangementsincludedforthecarriageofcontainers, withertanktopincreasedinthicknessto18mm, andstrengthenedtoallowamaximumpermissableloadingof15tonnes/m2andcontainerpointstackloadingof42tonnes. Thesingle62.40mx11.50mbox-shapedholdextendsintothe2.31mhighatchcoaming, andcanaccommodate102TEU, stowedinthreetiersandfourows, with48TEUcarriedonthepontoonhatchcoversinfourows, twotiershighathebridgefrontreducingtosingletierforward.
Twocorrugated-steel, single-wall, moveablebulkheadsprovideportablecargodivisionswhicharepositionedathetopbymeansofslotsinthehatchcoaming, andathebottomusingthetanktopcontainerfittings. Thesecanbevariouslyarrangedtosuitgrainandotherbulkcargoeswhich, alongwithsteelcoils, areamajorcomponentofArklow'stradingpattern.
Additionally, lashingeyesarearrangedintheholdsidestosuitprojectcargoes. Thehatchcoversandthemoveablebulkheadsarehandledbyatravellingcranewhichrunsalongthehatchcoamingandstowsathebridgefrontwhenotinuse. FacilitiesareincludedforthecarriageofdangerouscargoesinaccordancewithSOLASchapterII-2Regulation54, andehumidifyingandmechanicalholdventilationarrangementsarefitted.
Thehullformincorporatesaradiusedtransom, andfeaturesafullaftbodywhichisofparticularinterestforthetwofullyintegratedtunnels, portandstarboard, alignedfromthebilge-strakesaroundframe30, tothecentrelineofthevessel. Theseintersectjustabovethepropellerandimprovewaterflowtoit, particularlyinshallowater, andmaintainpropellerimmersion, evenindifficultweatherconditions. Thearrangementhasbeenadoptedbythebuilderinumerousdesignsandwhenfittedinconjunctionwithaflap-typerudderisaidtogivexcellentmanoeuvringperformance.
Thedoublehullstructurecontainseparatesideandbottomtanks, withthelatterdividedbyacentrelineductkeelcarryingthemainpipingsystems. Theseareservedbytwoballastpumps, twogeneralservicepumps (oneofwhichisfittedforwardinthebowthrusteroom), andthreejectors. Poopandforecastlerectionsareincluded, andabreakwaterbehindthelattergivesprotectiontocontainers. Accommodationisarrangedaftforeightpersons, occupyingthreedecksandfeaturingbulkheadsandceilingsinaccordancewithSOLASfireprotectionmethodI-C; A-60, A-30andA-0insulation; andfloatingfloorsandwainscotting.
ThemainengineisthesameasthatfittedinArklow
Rally: namelyanMaK6M25unitdeveloping1800kWat750rev/min, butdrivingthehigh-skewCPpropelleratahigher197rev/min, via reductiongearbox (bothgearboxandpropellerareprovidedbyScanaVoldaunderthelattercompany'spackageagreementwithMaK). APTOconnectswitha435kVAalternator, andtwo175kVAdiesel-drivenalternatorsarealsofitted, oneofwhichoperatesinemergency/harbourmodeandispositionedoutsidethengineroominthesuperstructure. A250kWthrusterisinstalledforward.

Thelatestrequirementsforhandlingballastinrestrictedwaters, andshipboardmanningpracticeshavebeenincorporated, aswellasregulationsgoverningpollution, safetyandcommunications. IceClass1Cclassificationrulesarealsocompliedwith.
Thevesselisdividedintosixcargoholdsbycorrugatedtransversebulkheads, andlaidoutwitholds1and4double-skinned. Thetanktopsarestrengthenedforheavycargoes, andthedesignisuitedformulti-portandblockloadingwithtwoholdslack, andforsailingin 'anyholdemptyHC-EA' conditions.

Theyareremotelycontrolledhydraulicallybyonepersonandsuppliedfromaseparatepowersystem.

Araisedforecastleand 'B' typefreeboardensuredrierdecksinloadedconditions, whilstself-trimmingrainloading, andstrengtheningagainstslammingatlightballastdraught (therebyreducingtheneedtoballastNo4hold), aresalientfeaturesofadesignaimedatincurringasfewrestrictionsaspossibleininternationaltrading. WithoperationsintheStLawrenceSeawaygivenspecialconsiderationinthisFortuneMkIIseries, abowthrusterassistsnavigationinrestrictedwatersandservestominimiseforwardshelldamage. Provisionforfittingpiping, valvesandcablesintheductkeelandsidepipetunnels, allowseasiermaintenance, andgivesprotectionagainstcorrosionandweatherconditions, forwhichpurposeballastanksareheated, andprovidedwithanair-bubblinganti-freezesystem.

Ballastingiscontrolledfromacentralstation, andautomationandmonitoringmeetsUMSandEOnotations. Totalnumberofsistershipsalreadycompleted:..............................Nil
Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: ........................................Nil FORmanyears, Kawasaki'snewbuildingoutputhasincludedvesselswhichdisplaytheyard'saccumulatedknowledgeofliquidgastransportationtechnology. Alargenumberofthesevesselsalsoincorporatetheresultsofthecompany'son-goingresearchintomarinehydrodynamics, andfeaturesuccessfulenergy-savingdevicesuchastheKawasakiRudderBulbSystem, typicallyfittedinconjunctionwithpropellerfins, contra-finsorsemi-ducts. CrystalMarinebenefitsfromthisadaptation, butismorespeciallynotableasthefirstvesseltoadoptKawasaki'slatesthull-formdevelopment, designatedthe 'SEA- Arrow' (anacronymfor 'Sharp-Entrance-AnglebowasanArrow').
LPGtankersareoftenrestrictedinlengthtosuitportfacilities, and, consequently, arebluff-bowed, so, tocompensate, cargotanksarextendedwellforwardinordertomaximisecargocapacity. Athigherspeeds, however, thischaracteristicproduceshighbowavesandincreasesresistance. Withthisinmind, Kawasakihasintroducedthisnewbowdesign, identifiedbyaverticalstem, inanattemptoreducetheproblemasappliedtoLPGtankers. Itdispenseswithtoday'snormal, bulbousbow, yetretainsthebeneficialeffectsofthatfeatureandisclaimedtohalvebow-resistancedrag, allowingthevesseltomaintainthesamespeedasa 'conventional-hull' LPGtankerofsimilarsize, butexpendingbetween5% and10% lesshorsepower, alternativelygaining0.3knots/0.5knotspeedincreasewhenoperatingathesamehorsepower.
CrystalMarineisaflush-deckedvessel, arrangedwithfourholdshavingtopsidewingtanks, andhoppersidetankswhicharecombinedwithcentrallydividedouble-bottomtanks. Allaremainlyutilisedforcarryingwaterballast. WhereasmostLPGcarriersofthisizeareconfiguredwithaforwardeeptanktosupplementheforepeakforballastingpurposes, thisdesignusesthenewbowhullformtoprovideonlyalargerforepeaktank.
